*Handler) SetReady(v ReadyStatus) {\n   643→\tif v == Ready {\n   644→\t\th.ready.Store(uint32(Ready))\n   645→\t\th.metrics.readyStatus.Set(1)\n   646→\t\treturn\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\th.ready.Store(uint32(v))\n   650→\th.metrics.readyStatus.Set(0)\n   651→}\n   652→\n   653→// Verifies whether the server is ready or not.\n   654→func (h *Handler) isReady() bool {\n   655→\treturn ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) == Ready\n   656→}\n   657→\n   658→// Checks if server is ready, calls f if it is, returns 503 if it is not.\n   659→func (h *Handler) testReady(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {\n   660→\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   661→\t\tswitch ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) {\n   662→\t\tcase Ready:\n   663→\t\t\tf(w, r)\n   664→\t\tcase NotReady:\n   665→\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"X-Prometheus-Stopping\", \"false\")\n   666→\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n   667→\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"Service Unavailable\")\n   668→\t\tcase Stopping:\n   669→\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"X-Prometheus-Stopping\", \"true\")\n   670→\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n   671→\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"Service Unavailable\")\n   672→\t\tdefault:\n   673→\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   674→\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"Unknown state\")\n   675→\t\t}\n   676→\t}\n   677→}\n   678→\n   679→// Quit returns the receive-only quit channel.\n   680→func (h *Handler) Quit() <-chan struct{} {\n   681→\treturn h.quitCh\n   682→}\n   683→\n   684→// Reload returns the receive-only channel requests.\n   690→func (h *Handler) Listeners() ([]net.Listener, error) {\n   691→\tvar listeners []net.Listener\n   692→\tsem := netconnlimit.NewSharedSemaphore(h.options.MaxConnections)\n   693→\tfor _, address := range h.options.ListenAddresses {\n   694→\t\tlistener, err := h.Listener(address, sem)\n   695→\t\tif err != nil {\n   696→\t\t\treturn listeners, err\n   697→\t\t}\n   698→\t\tlisteners = append(listeners, listener)\n   699→\t}\n   700→\treturn listeners, nil\n   701→}\n   702→\n   703→// Listener creates the TCP listener for web requests.\n   704→func (h *Handler) Listener(address string, sem chan struct{}) (net.Listener, error) {\n   705→\th.logger.Info(\"Start listening for connections\", \"address\", address)\n   706→\n   707→\tlistener, err := net.Listen(\"tcp\", address)\n   708→\tif err != nil {\n   709→\t\treturn listener, err\n   710→\t}\n   711→\tlistener = netconnlimit.SharedLimitListener(listener, sem)\n   712→\n   713→\t// Monitor incoming connections with conntrack.\n   714→\tlistener = conntrack.NewListener(listener,\n   715→\t\tconntrack.TrackWithName(\"http\"),\n   716→\t\tconntrack.TrackWithTracing())\n   717→\n   718→\treturn listener, nil\n   719→}\n   720→\n   721→// Run serves the HTTP endpoints.\n   722→func (h *Handler) Run(ctx context.Context, listeners []net.Listener, webConfig string) error {\n   723→\tif len(listeners) == 0 {\n   724→\t\tvar err error\n   725→\t\tlisteners, err = h.Listeners()\n   726→\t\tif err != nil {\n   727→\t\t\treturn err\n   728→\t\t}\n   729→\t}\n   730→\n   731→\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n   732→\tmux.Handle(\"/\", h.router)\n   733→\n   734→\tapiPath := \"/api\"\n   735→\tif h.options.RoutePrefix != \"/\" {\n   736→\t\tapiPath = h.options.RoutePrefix + apiPath\n   737→\t\th.logger.Info(\"Router prefix\", \"prefix\", h.options.RoutePrefix)\n   738→\t}\n   739→\tav1 := route.New().\n   740→\t\tWithInstrumentation(h.metrics.instrumentHandlerWithPrefix(\"/api/v1\")).\n   741→\t\tWithInstrumentation(setPathWithPrefix(apiPath + \"/v1\"))\n   742→\th.apiV1.Register(av1)\n   743→\n   744→\tmux.Handle(apiPath+\"/v1/\", http.StripPrefix(apiPath+\"/v1\", av1))\n   745→\n   746→\terrlog := slog.NewLogLogger(h.logger.Handler(), slog.LevelError)\n   747→\n   748→\tspanNameFormatter := otelhttp.WithSpanNameFormatter(func(_ string, r *http.Request) string {\n   749→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s\", r.Method, r.URL.Path)\n   750→\t})\n   751→\n   752→\thttpSrv := &http.Server{\n   753→\t\tHandler:     withStackTracer(otelhttp.NewHandler(mux, \"\", spanNameFormatter), h.logger),\n   754→\t\tErrorLog:    errlog,\n   755→\t\tReadTimeout: h.options.ReadTimeout,\n   756→\t}\n   757→\n   758→\terrCh := make(chan error, 1)\n   759→\tgo func() {\n   760→\t\terrCh <- toolkit_web.ServeMultiple(listeners, httpSrv, &toolkit_web.FlagConfig{WebConfigFile: &webConfig}, h.logger)\n   761→\t}()\n   762→\n   763→\tselect {\n   764→\tcase e := <-errCh:\n   765→\t\treturn e\n   766→\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   767→\t\thttpSrv.Shutdown(ctx)\n   768→\t\treturn nil\n   769→\t}\n   770→}\n   771→\n   772→func (h *Handler) consoles(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   773→\tctx := r.Context()\n   774→\tname := route.Param(ctx, \"filepath\")\n   775→\n   776→\tfile, err := http.Dir(h.options.ConsoleTemplatesPath).Open(name)\n   777→\tif err != nil {\n   778→\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusNotFound)\n   779→\t\treturn\n   780→\t}\n   781→\tdefer file.Close()\n   782→\ttext, err := io.ReadAll(file)\n   783→\tif err != nil {\n   784→\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   785→\t\treturn\n   786→\t}\n   787→\n   788→\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n   789→\n   790→\t// Provide URL parameters as a map for easy use. Advanced users may have need for\n   791→\t// parameters beyond the first, so provide RawParams.\n   792→\trawParams, err := url.ParseQuery(r.URL.RawQuery)\n   793→\tif err != nil {\n   794→\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)\n   795→\t\treturn\n   796→\t}\n   797→\tparams := map[string]string{}\n   798→\tfor k, v := range rawParams {\n   799→\t\tparams[k] = v[0]\n   800→\t}\n   801→\n   802→\th.mtx.RLock()\n   803→\tels := h.config.GlobalConfig.ExternalLabels\n   804→\th.mtx.RUnlock()\n   805→\texternalLabels := els.Map()\n   806→\n   807→\t// Inject some convenience variables that are easier to remember for users\n   808→\t// who are not used to Go's templating system.\n   809→\tdefs := []string{\n   810→\t\t\"{{$rawParams := .RawParams }}\",\n   811→\t\t\"{{$params := .Params}}\",\n   812→\t\t\"{{$path := .Path}}\",\n   813→\t\t\"{{$externalLabels := .ExternalLabels}}\",\n   814→\t}\n   815→\n   816→\tdata := struct {\n   817→\t\tRawParams      url.Values\n   818→\t\tParams         map[string]string\n   819→\t\tPath           string\n   820→\t\tExternalLabels map[string]string\n   821→\t}{\n   822→\t\tRawParams:      rawParams,\n   823→\t\tParams:         params,\n   824→\t\tPath:           strings.TrimLeft(name, \"/\"),\n   825→\t\tExternalLabels: externalLabels,\n   826→\t}\n   827→\n   828→\ttmpl := template.NewTemplateExpander(\n   829→\t\tctx,\n   830→\t\tstrings.Join(append(defs, string(text)), \"\"),\n   831→\t\t\"__console_\"+name,\n   832→\t\tdata,\n   833→\t\th.now(),\n   834→\t\ttemplate.QueryFunc(rules.EngineQueryFunc(h.queryEngine, h.storage)),\n   835→\t\th.options.ExternalURL,\n   836→\t\tnil,\n   837→\t)\n   838→\tfilenames, err := filepath.Glob(h.options.ConsoleLibrariesPath + \"/*.lib\")\n   839→\tif err != nil {\n   840→\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   841→\t\treturn\n   842→\t}\n   843→\tresult, err := tmpl.ExpandHTML(filenames)\n   844→\tif err != nil {\n   845→\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   846→\t\treturn\n   847→\t}\n   848→\tio.WriteString(w, result)\n   849→}\n   850→\n   851→func (h *Handler) runtimeInfo() (api_v1.RuntimeInfo, error) {\n   852→\tstatus := api_v1.RuntimeInfo{\n   853→\t\tStartTime:      h.birth,\n   854→\t\tCWD:            h.cwd,\n   855→\t\tGoroutineCount: runtime.NumGoroutine(),\n   856→\t\tGOMAXPROCS:     runtime.GOMAXPROCS(0),\n   857→\t\tGOMEMLIMIT:     debug.SetMemoryLimit(-1),\n   858→\t\tGOGC:           os.Getenv(\"GOGC\"),\n   859→\t\tGODEBUG:        os.Getenv(\"GODEBUG\"),\n   860→\t}\n   861→\n   862→\thostname, err := os.Hostname()\n   863→\tif err != nil {\n   864→\t\treturn status, fmt.Errorf(\"error getting hostname: %w\", err)\n   865→\t}\n   866→\tstatus.Hostname = hostname\n   867→\tstatus.ServerTime = time.Now().UTC()\n   868→\n   869→\tif h.options.TSDBRetentionDuration != 0 {\n   870→\t\tstatus.StorageRetention = h.options.TSDBRetentionDuration.String()\n   871→\t}\n   872→\tif h.options.TSDBMaxBytes != 0 {\n   873→\t\tif status.StorageRetention != \"\" {\n   874→\t\t\tstatus.StorageRetention += \" or \"\n   875→\t\t}\n   876→\t\tstatus.StorageRetention += h.options.TSDBMaxBytes.String()\n   877→\t}\n   878→\tif h.options.TSDBMaxPercentage != 0 {\n   879→\t\tif status.StorageRetention != \"\" {\n   880→\t\t\tstatus.StorageRetention += \" or \"\n   881→\t\t}\n   882→\t\tstatus.StorageRetention = status.StorageRetention + strconv.FormatUint(uint64(h.options.TSDBMaxPercentage), 10) + \"%\"\n   883→\t}\n   884→\n   885→\tmetrics, err := h.gatherer.Gather()\n   886→\tif err != nil {\n   887→\t\treturn status, fmt.Errorf(\"error gathering runtime status: %w\", err)\n   888→\t}\n   889→\tfor _, mF := range metrics {\n   890→\t\tswitch *mF.Name {\n   891→\t\tcase \"prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total\":\n   892→\t\t\tstatus.CorruptionCount = int64(toFloat64(mF))\n   893→\t\tcase \"prometheus_config_last_reload_successful\":\n   894→\t\t\tstatus.ReloadConfigSuccess = toFloat64(mF) != 0\n   895→\t\tcase \"prometheus_config_last_reload_success_timestamp_seconds\":\n   896→\t\t\tstatus.LastConfigTime =
